Although the hotel has been open for many years, there will be no mold in the room. Is it because the north is dry? This is the most satisfactory, because the southern hotel has been open for several years, and the maintenance is not good, and the room will basically have mold. The electric kettle is not clean and has black dirt

Service: Although the hygiene was not done carefully on the first day of check-in, the service attitude of the room sister was super good. The service speed was very fast when cleaning, changing and replenishing supplies. At breakfast, there was a shaved staff member who was very careful. The gentleman put his mobile phone on the table to watch videos, and he took the initiative to get a mobile phone holder.

Breakfast: Because I stayed for 6 days, the breakfast was almost the same every day, and I was tired of it. There was no Northeastern breakfast, and the Chinese breakfast was basically salty. Facilities: The socket on the water bar table was broken. It was my first time to the Northeast, and I felt that the floor heating temperature was very comfortable, and I could turn on the air conditioner to blow cool air. It was not like the southern hotels, where the central air conditioner was turned on in winter and it was dry, stuffy, and hot. The room was large, and the bathroom area was large, but the shower room was a little small, and the bath water temperature was unstable, a little hot and cold, but it was acceptable.
